[2026-01-04T04:06:54Z] Akshay: Y-derived products such as Z and A contain a high concentration of phyto-X, or X derived from plants. PhytoX are structurally and functionally very similar to human X. This is therefore the basis of a persistent concern B among people (especially men) who follow a certain lifestyle (or extremely funny consequence if you don’t subscribe to said lifestyle). Scientific evidence is extremely thin though, and the belief that typical Z or A consumption causes B is most likely a myth. PhytoX is much much less potent than human X and some studies show that you will need to consume some 3L of Z a day to show appreciable B, making it a remote possibility for most. Others also point out that conventional Z contains much more potent animal X, and yet doesnt generate as much concern. Give X, Y, Z, A, B.
